  <script>
   //load the apstag.js library (amazon prebid)
    !function (a9, a, p, s, t, A, g) { if (a[a9]) return; function q(c, r) { a[a9]._Q.push([c, r]) } a[a9] = { init: function () { q("i", arguments) }, fetchBids: function () { q("f", arguments) }, setDisplayBids: function () { }, targetingKeys: function () { return [] }, _Q: [] }; A = p.createElement(s); A.async = !0; A.src = t; g = p.getElementsByTagName(s)[0]; g.parentNode.insertBefore(A, g) }("apstag", window, document, "script", "//c.amazon-adsystem.com/aax2/apstag.js");

    //initialize the apstag.js library on the page to allow bidding
    apstag.init({
        pubID: '03086deb-b728-420a-9fad-35ee317c06f6', //enter your pub ID here as shown above, it must within quotes
        adServer: 'googletag'
    });


    var PREBID_IS_MOBILE = false;
    var PREBID_TIMEOUT = 1500;

    if (IS_SLOW_INTERNET === true)
        PREBID_TIMEOUT = 2000;

    var CONSENT_TIMEOUT = 1000;
    var FAILSAFE_TIMEOUT = 8000;
    var CURRENCY_RATE = 0.82;

    var requestManager = {
        adserverRequestSent: false,
        aps: false,
        prebid: false
    };


    var pbjs = pbjs || {};
    pbjs.que = pbjs.que || [];
    var adUnits = adUnits || [];
    var amazonAdSlots = amazonAdSlots || [];



    pbjs.bidderSettings = {
        rubicon: {
            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm) {
                return bidCpm * CURRENCY_RATE;
            }
        },
        criteo: {
            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm) {
                return bidCpm * CURRENCY_RATE;
            }
        },
        ix: {
            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm) {
                return bidCpm * CURRENCY_RATE;
            }
        },
        appnexus: {
            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm) {
                return bidCpm * CURRENCY_RATE;
            }
        },
        connectad: {
            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm) {
                return bidCpm * CURRENCY_RATE;
            }
        },
        adform: {
            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm) {
                return bidCpm; //* CURRENCY_RATE; removing currency rate, as requested for adform
            }
        },
        openx: {
            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm) {
                return bidCpm * CURRENCY_RATE;
            }
        },
        smartadserver: {
            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm) {
                return bidCpm * CURRENCY_RATE;
            }
        },
        luponmedia: {
            bidCpmAdjustment: function (bidCpm) {
                return bidCpm * CURRENCY_RATE;
            }
        }
    };

    const customPrebidGranularity = {
        "buckets": [
            {
                "min": 0,
                "max": 100,
                "increment": 0.01
            }
        ]
    };


    var googletag = googletag || {};
    googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
    });


    window.didomiEventListeners = window.didomiEventListeners || [];
    window.didomiEventListeners.push({
        event: 'integrations.consentpassedtodfp',
        listener: function (data) {
            // Consent has been passed to Google
            // Load or refresh ads as needed with DFP, Prebid, etc.
            // `data.consentStatus` contains the current consent status of the user (true/false/undefined)
            // `data.index` contains the index of the event (integer)
            if (data.index === 0) {
                // This is the very first event on the page that gets triggered on page load
                initializeGoogletagRefreshWithPrebid();
            } else {
                // This is an event that happens later on the page, after a user action (user giving consent or changing their preferences)
                //googletag.pubads().refresh();
            }
        }
    });




    function initializeGoogletagRefreshWithPrebid() {
        //amazon init
        // APS request
        if (amazonAdSlots.length > 0) {
            apstag.fetchBids({
                slots: amazonAdSlots
            }, function (bids) {
                googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                    apstag.setDisplayBids();
                    requestManager.aps = true; // signals that APS request has completed
                    biddersBack(); // checks whether both APS and Prebid have returned
                });
            });
        }
        else {
            requestManager.aps = true; // signals that APS request has completed
            biddersBack(); // checks whether both APS and Prebid have returned
        }

        //prebid init
        pbjs.que.push(function () {

            pbjs.setConfig({
                consentManagement: {
                    cmpApi: 'iab',
                    timeout: CONSENT_TIMEOUT,
                    allowAuctionWithoutConsent: true,
                    defaultGdprScope: true
                },
                //debug: true,
                userSync: {
                    filterSettings: {
                        iframe: {
                            bidders: '*',      // '*' represents all bidders
                            filter: 'include'
                        }
                    }
                },
                priceGranularity: customPrebidGranularity,
                enableSendAllBids: true
            });

            pbjs.addAdUnits(adUnits);
            pbjs.requestBids({
                bidsBackHandler: function () {
                    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                        pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();
                        requestManager.prebid = true; // signals that Prebid request has completed
                        biddersBack(); // checks whether both APS and Prebid have returned
                    })
                },
                timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT
            });
        });
    }


    // when both APS and Prebid have returned, initiate ad request
    function biddersBack() {
        if (requestManager.aps && requestManager.prebid) {
            sendAdserverRequest();
        }
        return;
    }


    function sendAdserverRequest() {
        if (requestManager.adserverRequestSent === true) {
            return;
        }
        requestManager.adserverRequestSent = true;

        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            pbjs.que.push(function () {

                var pbInterval = setInterval(function () {

                    //when ads are available, refresh it
                    if (googletag.pubads().getSlots().length > 0) {
                        console.log('pbjs callback')
                        clearInterval(pbInterval); //clear interval for ad render (should trigger only once)

                        googletag.enableServices();
                        googletag.pubads().refresh();
                        console.log('refreshed')
                    }

                }, 10);
            });
        });
    }

    //in case PBJS doesn't load
    setTimeout(function () {
        sendAdserverRequest();
    }, FAILSAFE_TIMEOUT);
  </script>

        ga('send', 'event', "ab_fifty-fifty", '');

        // if ad block detected send event
        if (window.indexCanRunAds === undefined) {
            ga('send', 'event', "ad_block_detected", 'true');
        }

        imageLazyLoadService.Init();
        globalDirectives.InitAll();
        layoutService.InitAll();
  </script>
